11b2(1): b+ha ba ha/ 'ong byon nas rigs kyi bu 'ji ga rten gyi khams me tog gi gzhi'i snying po'i rgyan bkod pa de dang / rgyal po dbang sgyur gyi khang pa chen po der/ bcom

12b2(1): pa'i rdo rje chen po'i pad+mo la 'dug go// nub byang gi phyogs mtshams na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs

12b5(1): mu khe d+hA/ sarba ta thA ga ta/ badz+ra kA ra niri go kha bo kraR+sha tha swA hA/ 'di byin nas btang ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po

13b1(1): rten gyi kharnams me tog gi gna'o snying po'i rgyan bkod pa gal ba dang / rgyal ba dbang sgyur gyi khang pa chen po gal ba dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dam
13b2(1): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad ga la ba der song nas/ bcom ldan 'das la len brgya stong phrag du mar bskor ba byas te/ ji ltar

14a7(1): dang bral zhing / nam mkha' ltar bzod mi nas zhi ba dang / yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po chen ltar bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pa yang mthong nas/

293a5(1): gro bas dbang bskur rim par bya// de nas mchod pa lnga dag gis// mchod pa lus la rgyas par mchod// yang dag bsgrub pa gang yin// phyag rgya bcas pas bsdogs pa yin// 
293a6(1): sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // bla ma rdo rje 'dzin pa la// gus pa'i yis ni sangs rgyas bde// mchod pa rab tu rgyas pa la// sngon du bsten pa yang dag bsgrub// khams gsum
293a7(1): rnam rgyal khro bo la// bsgrub pa'i thabs 'di yang dag sbyang // gang gi cha byad de nyid la dur khrod dag tu song byas la// mo yi thal ba gang yin pas// bdag nyid lus la khyab par byug
293b1(1): g.yon du thod pa thogs byas la// g.yas su rdo rje thogs byas te// rin chen dkar po'i 'phreng ba las// drag po bzlas pa mang du bya// de'i langs spyod pas bza' zhing // stag gi lpags
293b2(1): pas smad bkris bya// don dang ldan pa'i snying po bsam// khrag gang yang bsku byas la// nag por gtogs pa'i 'phro ba brgyad// sol ba'i me la zhugs byas la// skar ma dag la nges pa
293b3(1): bsgom chang 'dra ba la gnas bcas la// shes rab bzung du ldan pa yis// skar ma nyid du mnyam sbyar la// brgyung pa yis ni sngags bzlas bya// zhags drangs phyag rgya brgyan pa yas
293b4(1): yang dag pa ru bsgrub par bya// de nas zhags grangs thom pa dang // mtha' ru mtshan mo thog thag par// sngags dag nges par bzlas par bya// de nas ske tshe yus kar dang // khra ga dang de
293b5(1): ngag sbyar ba yis// spyon bsreg stong du thim byas la// ka ra wI ra'i lcug ma la// tsan dan dmar po'i chus bkus te// me tog 'phreng bas btab po yis// lag pa g.yas pas thog
293b6(1): byas te// yid ches sprul thag pa yis// yang dag bcu bkal nas ni// bdag gi skyo bar yongs su bcing // de nas grong khyer dkyus pa na// kun gyis phyag byed mchod pa byed/ 
293b7(1): 'jig rten kun gyis phyag byed cing // snying du sdug pa nges pa yin// mkha' 'gro la sogs phramanams// bdag la lung yang nges par ston// sdug bsngal rtag tu mi 'byung zhing / 
294a1(1): lha man la sogs gdug pa yis// me'i phung po mthong ba yon// bdag la sdig pa dmar pos 'jus// de la 'dzags pa bskyed mi bya// bdag la bdug pa sna tshogs pa// gnod
294a2(1): pa sna tshogs byed pa ni// de la 'dzags pa mi bskyed cing // sems dga' ba yis yongs su mchod// o ka pa la d+ha ra sen d+ha yi// oM bak+Sha sa R+Ya na ma sa naM// hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ 
294a3(1): oM d+ha ka bya ba ga Shi ka ra ya swA hA// oM sarba lo kau pra shi kA ra ya hUM// oM sar+b+ba duSh+Ta tsad tA na sa na ya phaT// oM ma hA ka pA sa pa ya hUM phaT// lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can rdo rje me lce'i rgyud las// 
294a4(1): tshangs pa srin po rnon 'dul ba'i le'u ste// bcu gnyis pa'o// // lag na rdo rje gos sngon gyis// bcom ldan mgon la 'di skad gsol// gang zhig gshin rjes zin pa la// tho bas de gang
294a5(1): gis sman pa lags// rig pa'i rgyal pos bka' stsal pa// gshin rje brang dmer zhes bya'i gdon// kha dog sngon po nyid le ni// mche ba bzhi dang rab ldan pa'i// g.yas pa thong dbyug
294a6(1): 'dzin pa la// g.yon pas mi'i mgon po 'dzim// drag po 'jigs su rung bal+lI// gdon gros gang dag zin gyur pa// thabs 'di gang dag sbyor ba bya// bdag gi sbyor bas bzung byas nas/ 
294a7(1): drug pa ska ldan tsan pa// shin tu dpa' ning dang pa ldan// stobs ldan gtim pa'i bdag cid can// zhag drug pa rang bsnyen bya ba// kha lA la sogs chang byin la// de la sngags kyi sangs
